  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'OnlineCourse' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'OnlineCourse' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse and enroll in courses, submit assignments, track progress, and receive certificates. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'OnlineCourse' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'OnlineCourse' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Learning Dashboard - **Overview**: Main hub displaying enrolled courses and progress. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying user's name.   - **ID: enrolled-courses** - Type: Div - Display of currently enrolled courses.   - **ID: browse-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to course catalog.   - **ID: my-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to my courses page.  ### 2. Course Catalog Page - **Page Title**: Available Courses - **Overview**: Browse all available courses. - **Elements**:   - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search courses.   - **ID: course-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of course cards.   - **ID: view-course-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - View course details. (Repeated Element)   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.  ### 3. Course Details Page - **Page Title**: Course Details - **Overview**: Detailed information about a course including syllabus and enrollment option. - **Elements**:   - **ID: course-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course details page.   - **ID: course-title** - Type: H1 - Display of course title.   - **ID: course-description** - Type: Div - Full description of course content.   - **ID: enroll-button** - Type: Button - Button to enroll in the course.   - **ID: back-to-catalog** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to course catalog. - **Functionality**:   - Enroll button creates entry in enrollments.txt with 0% initial progress   - If already enrolled, button shows "Already Enrolled" and is disabled   - Enrollment date is recorded as current date  ### 4. My Courses Page - **Page Title**: My Courses - **Overview**: Display enrolled courses and progress. - **Elements**:   - **ID: my-courses-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my courses page.   - **ID: courses-list** - Type: Div - List of enrolled courses with progress.   - **ID: continue-learning-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - Continue learning a course. (Repeated Element)   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.  ### 5. Course Learning Page - **Page Title**: Course Learning - **Overview**: View course content and lessons with progress tracking. - **Elements**:   - **ID: learning-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course learning page.   - **ID: lessons-list** - Type: Div - List of all lessons in the course.   - **ID: lesson-content** - Type: Div - Display of current lesson materials.   - **ID: mark-complete-button** - Type: Button - Button to mark current lesson as completed.   - **ID: back-to-my-courses** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to enrolled courses. - **Functionality**:   - Progress is calculated as (completed lessons / total lessons) × 100   - Marking lesson complete updates enrollments.txt progress field   - Course completion (100% progress) automatically generates certificate   - Lessons must be completed in sequence  ### 6. My Assignments Page - **Page Title**: My Assignments - **Overview**: View and submit assignments. - **Elements**:   - **ID: assignments-page** - Type: Div - Container for assignments page.   - **ID: assignments-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all assignments.   - **ID: submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id}** - Type: Button - Submit a pending assignment. (Repeated Element)   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Submit Assignment Page - **Page Title**: Submit Assignment - **Overview**: Submit assignment work with text responses. - **Elements**:   - **ID: submit-page** - Type: Div - Container for the assignment submission page.   - **ID: assignment-info** - Type: Div - Display of assignment title and description.   - **ID: submission-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to input text response.   - **ID: submit-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the assignment.   - **ID: back-to-assignments** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to assignments list. - **Functionality**:   - Submission creates entry in submissions.txt with status "Submitted"   - Submit date is recorded for late submission tracking   - Confirmation message displays after successful submission  ### 8. Certificates Page - **Page Title**: My Certificates - **Overview**: View earned course completion certificates. - **Elements**:   - **ID: certificates-page** - Type: Div - Container for the certificates page.   - **ID: certificates-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of certificate cards.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard. - **Functionality**:   - Certificates are automatically generated when course progress reaches 100%   - Certificate entry is added to certificates.txt with current date   - Only completed courses appear in the grid  ### 9. User Profile Page - **Page Title**: My Profile - **Overview**: View and edit profile. - **Elements**:   - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for profile page.   - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Email input field.   - **ID: profile-fullname** - Type: Input - Full name input field.   - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Save profile changes.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'OnlineCourse' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**: `username|email|fullname` - **Example Data**:   ```   john|john@student.com|John Student   alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor   jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner   ```  ### 2. Courses Data - **File Name**: `courses.txt` - **Data Format**: `course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active   2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active   3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active   ```  ### 3. Enrollments Data - **File Name**: `enrollments.txt` - **Data Format**: `enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress   2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed   3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress   ```  ### 4. Assignments Data - **File Name**: `assignments.txt` - **Data Format**: `assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100   2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200   ```  ### 5. Submissions Data - **File Name**: `submissions.txt` - **Data Format**: `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!   2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!   ```  ### 6. Certificates Data - **File Name**: `certificates.txt` - **Data Format**: `certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|jane|1|2024-11-22   ```

# Requirements Document for 'OnlineCourse' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'OnlineCourse' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse and enroll in courses, submit assignments, track progress, and receive certificates. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'OnlineCourse' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'OnlineCourse' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Learning Dashboard
- **Overview**: Main hub displaying enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying user's name.
  - **ID: enrolled-courses** - Type: Div - Display of currently enrolled courses.
  - **ID: browse-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to course catalog.
  - **ID: my-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to my courses page.

### 2. Course Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Available Courses
- **Overview**: Browse all available courses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search courses.
  - **ID: course-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of course cards.
  - **ID: view-course-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - View course details. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Course Details Page
- **Page Title**: Course Details
- **Overview**: Detailed information about a course including syllabus and enrollment option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: course-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course details page.
  - **ID: course-title** - Type: H1 - Display of course title.
  - **ID: course-description** - Type: Div - Full description of course content.
  - **ID: enroll-button** - Type: Button - Button to enroll in the course.
  - **ID: back-to-catalog** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to course catalog.
- **Functionality**:
  - Enroll button creates entry in enrollments.txt with 0% initial progress
  - If already enrolled, button shows "Already Enrolled" and is disabled
  - Enrollment date is recorded as current date

### 4. My Courses Page
- **Page Title**: My Courses
- **Overview**: Display enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-courses-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my courses page.
  - **ID: courses-list** - Type: Div - List of enrolled courses with progress.
  - **ID: continue-learning-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - Continue learning a course. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Course Learning Page
- **Page Title**: Course Learning
- **Overview**: View course content and lessons with progress tracking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: learning-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course learning page.
  - **ID: lessons-list** - Type: Div - List of all lessons in the course.
  - **ID: lesson-content** - Type: Div - Display of current lesson materials.
  - **ID: mark-complete-button** - Type: Button - Button to mark current lesson as completed.
  - **ID: back-to-my-courses** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to enrolled courses.
- **Functionality**:
  - Progress is calculated as (completed lessons / total lessons) × 100
  - Marking lesson complete updates enrollments.txt progress field
  - Course completion (100% progress) automatically generates certificate
  - Lessons must be completed in sequence

### 6. My Assignments Page
- **Page Title**: My Assignments
- **Overview**: View and submit assignments.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: assignments-page** - Type: Div - Container for assignments page.
  - **ID: assignments-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all assignments.
  - **ID: submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id}** - Type: Button - Submit a pending assignment. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Submit Assignment Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Assignment
- **Overview**: Submit assignment work with text responses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: submit-page** - Type: Div - Container for the assignment submission page.
  - **ID: assignment-info** - Type: Div - Display of assignment title and description.
  - **ID: submission-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to input text response.
  - **ID: submit-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the assignment.
  - **ID: back-to-assignments** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to assignments list.
- **Functionality**:
  - Submission creates entry in submissions.txt with status "Submitted"
  - Submit date is recorded for late submission tracking
  - Confirmation message displays after successful submission

### 8. Certificates Page
- **Page Title**: My Certificates
- **Overview**: View earned course completion certificates.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: certificates-page** - Type: Div - Container for the certificates page.
  - **ID: certificates-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of certificate cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
- **Functionality**:
  - Certificates are automatically generated when course progress reaches 100%
  - Certificate entry is added to certificates.txt with current date
  - Only completed courses appear in the grid

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: View and edit profile.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for profile page.
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Email input field.
  - **ID: profile-fullname** - Type: Input - Full name input field.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'OnlineCourse' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**: `username|email|fullname`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john|john@student.com|John Student
  alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor
  jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner
  ```

### 2. Courses Data
- **File Name**: `courses.txt`
- **Data Format**: `course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active
  ```

### 3. Enrollments Data
- **File Name**: `enrollments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress
  ```

### 4. Assignments Data
- **File Name**: `assignments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200
  ```

### 5. Submissions Data
- **File Name**: `submissions.txt`
- **Data Format**: `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!
  ```

### 6. Certificates Data
- **File Name**: `certificates.txt`
- **Data Format**: `certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane|1|2024-11-22
  ```

# Requirements Document for 'OnlineCourse' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'OnlineCourse' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse and enroll in courses, submit assignments, track progress, and receive certificates. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'OnlineCourse' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'OnlineCourse' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Learning Dashboard
- **Overview**: Main hub displaying enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying user's name.
  - **ID: enrolled-courses** - Type: Div - Display of currently enrolled courses.
  - **ID: browse-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to course catalog.
  - **ID: my-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to my courses page.

### 2. Course Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Available Courses
- **Overview**: Browse all available courses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search courses.
  - **ID: course-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of course cards.
  - **ID: view-course-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - View course details. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Course Details Page
- **Page Title**: Course Details
- **Overview**: Detailed information about a course including syllabus and enrollment option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: course-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course details page.
  - **ID: course-title** - Type: H1 - Display of course title.
  - **ID: course-description** - Type: Div - Full description of course content.
  - **ID: enroll-button** - Type: Button - Button to enroll in the course.
  - **ID: back-to-catalog** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to course catalog.
- **Functionality**:
  - Enroll button creates entry in enrollments.txt with 0% initial progress
  - If already enrolled, button shows "Already Enrolled" and is disabled
  - Enrollment date is recorded as current date

### 4. My Courses Page
- **Page Title**: My Courses
- **Overview**: Display enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-courses-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my courses page.
  - **ID: courses-list** - Type: Div - List of enrolled courses with progress.
  - **ID: continue-learning-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - Continue learning a course. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Course Learning Page
- **Page Title**: Course Learning
- **Overview**: View course content and lessons with progress tracking.

  - **ID: learning-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course learning page.

  - Progress is calculated as (completed lessons / total lessons) × 100
  - Marking lesson complete updates enrollments.txt progress field
  - Course completion (100% progress) automatically generates certificate
  - Lessons must be completed in sequence

### 6. My Assignments Page
- **Page Title**: My Assignments
- **Overview**: View and submit assignments.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: assignments-page** - Type: Div - Container for assignments page.
  - **ID: assignments-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all assignments.
  - **ID: submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id}** - Type: Button - Submit a pending assignment. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Submit Assignment Page

  - **ID: assignment-info** - Type: Div - Display of assignment title and description.
  - **ID: submission-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to input text response.
  - **ID: submit-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the assignment.
  - **ID: back-to-assignments** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to assignments list.

  - Submit date is recorded for late submission tracking
  - Confirmation message displays after successful submission

## 4. Data Storage

The 'OnlineCourse' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**: `username|email|fullname`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john|john@student.com|John Student
  alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor
  jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner
  ```

### 2. Courses Data
- **File Name**: `courses.txt`
- **Data Format**: `course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active
  ```

### 3. Enrollments Data
- **File Name**: `enrollments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress
  ```

### 4. Assignments Data
- **File Name**: `assignments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200
  ```

### 5. Submissions Data
- **File Name**: `submissions.txt`
- **Data Format**: `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!
  ```

### 6. Certificates Data
- **File Name**: `certificates.txt`
- **Data Format**: `certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane|1|2024-11-22
  ```

# Requirements Document for 'OnlineCourse' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'OnlineCourse' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse and enroll in courses, submit assignments, track progress, and receive certificates. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'OnlineCourse' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'OnlineCourse' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Learning Dashboard
- **Overview**: Main hub displaying enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying user's name.
  - **ID: enrolled-courses** - Type: Div - Display of currently enrolled courses.
  - **ID: browse-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to course catalog.
  - **ID: my-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to my courses page.

### 2. Course Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Available Courses
- **Overview**: Browse all available courses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search courses.
  - **ID: course-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of course cards.
  - **ID: view-course-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - View course details. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Course Details Page
- **Page Title**: Course Details
- **Overview**: Detailed information about a course including syllabus and enrollment option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: course-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course details page.
  - **ID: course-title** - Type: H1 - Display of course title.
  - **ID: course-description** - Type: Div - Full description of course content.
  - **ID: enroll-button** - Type: Button - Button to enroll in the course.
  - **ID: back-to-catalog** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to course catalog.
- **Functionality**:
  - Enroll button creates entry in enrollments.txt with 0% initial progress
  - If already enrolled, button shows "Already Enrolled" and is disabled
  - Enrollment date is recorded as current date

### 4. My Courses Page
- **Page Title**: My Courses
- **Overview**: Display enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-courses-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my courses page.
  - **ID: courses-list** - Type: Div - List of enrolled courses with progress.
  - **ID: continue-learning-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - Continue learning a course. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Course Learning Page
- **Page Title**: Course Learning
- **Overview**: View course content and lessons with progress tracking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: learning-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course learning page.
  - **ID: lessons-list** - Type: Div - List of all lessons in the course.
  - **ID: lesson-content** - Type: Div - Display of current lesson materials.
  - **ID: mark-complete-button** - Type: Button - Button to mark current lesson as completed.
  - **ID: back-to-my-courses** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to enrolled courses.
- **Functionality**:
  - Progress is calculated as (completed lessons / total lessons) × 100
  - Marking lesson complete updates enrollments.txt progress field
  - Course completion (100% progress) automatically generates certificate
  - Lessons must be completed in sequence

### 6. My Assignments Page
- **Page Title**: My Assignments
- **Overview**: View and submit assignments.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: assignments-page** - Type: Div - Container for assignments page.
  - **ID: assignments-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all assignments.
  - **ID: submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id}** - Type: Button - Submit a pending assignment. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Submit Assignment Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Assignment
- **Overview**: Submit assignment work with text responses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: submit-page** - Type: Div - Container for the assignment submission page.
  - **ID: assignment-info** - Type: Div - Display of assignment title and description.
  - **ID: submission-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to input text response.
  - **ID: submit-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the assignment.
  - **ID: back-to-assignments** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to assignments list.
- **Functionality**:
  - Submission creates entry in submissions.txt with status "Submitted"
  - Submit date is recorded for late submission tracking
  - Confirmation message displays after successful submission

### 8. Certificates Page
- **Page Title**: My Certificates
- **Overview**: View earned course completion certificates.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: certificates-page** - Type: Div - Container for the certificates page.
  - **ID: certificates-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of certificate cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
- **Functionality**:
  - Certificates are automatically generated when course progress reaches 100%
  - Certificate entry is added to certificates.txt with current date
  - Only completed courses appear in the grid

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: View and edit profile.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for profile page.
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Email input field.
  - **ID: profile-fullname** - Type: Input - Full name input field.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'OnlineCourse' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**: `username|email|fullname`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john|john@student.com|John Student
  alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor
  jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner
  ```

### 2. Courses Data
- **File Name**: `courses.txt`
- **Data Format**: `course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active
  ```

### 3. Enrollments Data
- **File Name**: `enrollments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress
  ```

### 4. Assignments Data
- **File Name**: `assignments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200
  ```

### 5. Submissions Data
- **File Name**: `submissions.txt`
- **Data Format**: `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!
  ```

### 6. Certificates Data
- **File Name**: `certificates.txt`
- **Data Format**: `certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane|1|2024-11-22
  ```

# Requirements Document for 'OnlineCourse' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'OnlineCourse' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse and enroll in courses, submit assignments, track progress, and receive certificates. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'OnlineCourse' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'OnlineCourse' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Learning Dashboard
- **Overview**: Main hub displaying enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying user's name.
  - **ID: enrolled-courses** - Type: Div - Display of currently enrolled courses.
  - **ID: browse-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to course catalog.
  - **ID: my-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to my courses page.

### 2. Course Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Available Courses
- **Overview**: Browse all available courses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search courses.
  - **ID: course-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of course cards.
  - **ID: view-course-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - View course details. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Course Details Page
- **Page Title**: Course Details
- **Overview**: Detailed information about a course including syllabus and enrollment option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: course-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course details page.
  - **ID: course-title** - Type: H1 - Display of course title.
  - **ID: course-description** - Type: Div - Full description of course content.
  - **ID: enroll-button** - Type: Button - Button to enroll in the course.
  - **ID: back-to-catalog** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to course catalog.
- **Functionality**:
  - Enroll button creates entry in enrollments.txt with 0% initial progress
  - If already enrolled, button shows "Already Enrolled" and is disabled
  - Enrollment date is recorded as current date

### 4. My Courses Page
- **Page Title**: My Courses
- **Overview**: Display enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-courses-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my courses page.
  - **ID: courses-list** - Type: Div - List of enrolled courses with progress.
  - **ID: continue-learning-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - Continue learning a course. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Course Learning Page
- **Page Title**: Course Learning
- **Overview**: View course content and lessons with progress tracking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: learning-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course learning page.
  - **ID: lessons-list** - Type: Div - List of all lessons in the course.
  - **ID: lesson-content** - Type: Div - Display of current lesson materials.
  - **ID: mark-complete-button** - Type: Button - Button to mark current lesson as completed.
  - **ID: back-to-my-courses** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to enrolled courses.
- **Functionality**:
  - Progress is calculated as (completed lessons / total lessons) × 100
  - Marking lesson complete updates enrollments.txt progress field
  - Course completion (100% progress) automatically generates certificate
  - Lessons must be completed in sequence

### 6. My Assignments Page
- **Page Title**: My Assignments
- **Overview**: View and submit assignments.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: assignments-page** - Type: Div - Container for assignments page.
  - **ID: assignments-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all assignments.
  - **ID: submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id}** - Type: Button - Submit a pending assignment. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Submit Assignment Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Assignment
- **Overview**: Submit assignment work with text responses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: submit-page** - Type: Div - Container for the assignment submission page.
  - **ID: assignment-info** - Type: Div - Display of assignment title and description.
  - **ID: submission-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to input text response.
  - **ID: submit-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the assignment.
  - **ID: back-to-assignments** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to assignments list.
- **Functionality**:
  - Submission creates entry in submissions.txt with status "Submitted"
  - Submit date is recorded for late submission tracking
  - Confirmation message displays after successful submission

### 8. Certificates Page
- **Page Title**: My Certificates
- **Overview**: View earned course completion certificates.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: certificates-page** - Type: Div - Container for the certificates page.
  - **ID: certificates-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of certificate cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
- **Functionality**:
  - Certificates are automatically generated when course progress reaches 100%
  - Certificate entry is added to certificates.txt with current date
  - Only completed courses appear in the grid

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: View and edit profile.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for profile page.
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Email input field.
  - **ID: profile-fullname** - Type: Input - Full name input field.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'OnlineCourse' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**: `username|email|fullname`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john|john@student.com|John Student
  alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor
  jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner
  ```

### 2. Courses Data
- **File Name**: `courses.txt`
- **Data Format**: `course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active
  ```

### 3. Enrollments Data
- **File Name**: `enrollments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress
  ```

### 4. Assignments Data
- **File Name**: `assignments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200
  ```

### 5. Submissions Data
- **File Name**: `submissions.txt`
- **Data Format**: `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!
  ```

### 6. Certificates Data
- **File Name**: `certificates.txt`
- **Data Format**: `certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane|1|2024-11-22
  ```

# Requirements Document for 'OnlineCourse' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'OnlineCourse' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse and enroll in courses, submit assignments, track progress, and receive certificates. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'OnlineCourse' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'OnlineCourse' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Learning Dashboard
- **Overview**: Main hub displaying enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying user's name.
  - **ID: enrolled-courses** - Type: Div - Display of currently enrolled courses.
  - **ID: browse-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to course catalog.
  - **ID: my-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to my courses page.

### 2. Course Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Available Courses
- **Overview**: Browse all available courses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search courses.
  - **ID: course-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of course cards.
  - **ID: view-course-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - View course details. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Course Details Page
- **Page Title**: Course Details
- **Overview**: Detailed information about a course including syllabus and enrollment option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: course-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course details page.
  - **ID: course-title** - Type: H1 - Display of course title.
  - **ID: course-description** - Type: Div - Full description of course content.
  - **ID: enroll-button** - Type: Button - Button to enroll in the course.
  - **ID: back-to-catalog** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to course catalog.
- **Functionality**:
  - Enroll button creates entry in enrollments.txt with 0% initial progress
  - If already enrolled, button shows "Already Enrolled" and is disabled
  - Enrollment date is recorded as current date

### 4. My Courses Page
- **Page Title**: My Courses
- **Overview**: Display enrolled courses and progress.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-courses-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my courses page.
  - **ID: courses-list** - Type: Div - List of enrolled courses with progress.
  - **ID: continue-learning-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - Continue learning a course. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Course Learning Page
- **Page Title**: Course Learning
- **Overview**: View course content and lessons with progress tracking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: learning-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course learning page.
  - **ID: lessons-list** - Type: Div - List of all lessons in the course.
  - **ID: lesson-content** - Type: Div - Display of current lesson materials.
  - **ID: mark-complete-button** - Type: Button - Button to mark current lesson as completed.
  - **ID: back-to-my-courses** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to enrolled courses.
- **Functionality**:
  - Progress is calculated as (completed lessons / total lessons) × 100
  - Marking lesson complete updates enrollments.txt progress field
  - Course completion (100% progress) automatically generates certificate
  - Lessons must be completed in sequence

### 6. My Assignments Page
- **Page Title**: My Assignments
- **Overview**: View and submit assignments.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: assignments-page** - Type: Div - Container for assignments page.
  - **ID: assignments-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all assignments.
  - **ID: submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id}** - Type: Button - Submit a pending assignment. (Repeated Element)
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Submit Assignment Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Assignment
- **Overview**: Submit assignment work with text responses.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: submit-page** - Type: Div - Container for the assignment submission page.
  - **ID: assignment-info** - Type: Div - Display of assignment title and description.
  - **ID: submission-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to input text response.
  - **ID: submit-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the assignment.
  - **ID: back-to-assignments** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to assignments list.
- **Functionality**:
  - Submission creates entry in submissions.txt with status "Submitted"
  - Submit date is recorded for late submission tracking
  - Confirmation message displays after successful submission

### 8. Certificates Page
- **Page Title**: My Certificates
- **Overview**: View earned course completion certificates.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: certificates-page** - Type: Div - Container for the certificates page.
  - **ID: certificates-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of certificate cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.
- **Functionality**:
  - Certificates are automatically generated when course progress reaches 100%
  - Certificate entry is added to certificates.txt with current date
  - Only completed courses appear in the grid

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: View and edit profile.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for profile page.
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Email input field.
  - **ID: profile-fullname** - Type: Input - Full name input field.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'OnlineCourse' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**: `username|email|fullname`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john|john@student.com|John Student
  alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor
  jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner
  ```

### 2. Courses Data
- **File Name**: `courses.txt`
- **Data Format**: `course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active
  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active
  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active
  ```

### 3. Enrollments Data
- **File Name**: `enrollments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress
  2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed
  3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress
  ```

### 4. Assignments Data
- **File Name**: `assignments.txt`
- **Data Format**: `assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100
  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200
  ```

### 5. Submissions Data
- **File Name**: `submissions.txt`
- **Data Format**: `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!
  ```

### 6. Certificates Data
- **File Name**: `certificates.txt`
- **Data Format**: `certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date`
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane|1|2024-11-22
  ```

- **Data Format**: `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback`

  ```
  1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!
  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!
  ```

# OnlineCourse Application Design Specification

This document provides detailed design specifications for the "OnlineCourse" Flask web application. It covers Flask Routes, HTML Template Specifications, and Data Schemas to enable independent backend and frontend development.

---

# Section 1: Flask Routes Specifications

| Route URL                  | Function Name            | HTTP Method | Description                                   | Context Variables                                                                                                    |
|----------------------------|--------------------------|-------------|-----------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `/dashboard`               | `dashboard`              | GET         | Displays user's learning dashboard             | `user_name` (str): Full name of logged-in user<br>`enrollments` (list of dict): Each dict with:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `course_title` (str)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `progress` (int percent) |
| `/courses`                 | `available_courses`      | GET         | Shows all available courses                     | `courses` (list of dict): Each dict with:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `course_id` (int)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `title` (str)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `description` (str)                             |
| `/course/<int:course_id>` | `course_details`         | GET         | Details of a selected course & enrollment status| `course` (dict):<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `course_id`, `title`, `description` (str)<br>`enrolled` (bool)<br>`enrollment_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD if enrolled)<br>`progress` (int)       |
| `/enroll/<int:course_id>` | `enroll`                 | POST/GET    | Enroll user in a course                         | Redirect to `/dashboard` or `/course/<course_id>` based on success                                                   |
| `/my-courses`             | `my_courses`             | GET         | List of user enrolled courses and progress     | `my_courses` (list of dict): Each dict with:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `course_id` (int)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `title` (str)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `progress` (int)                               |
| `/learning/<int:course_id>` | `learning_page`           | GET         | Display lessons of a course with progress       | `course_id` (int)<br>`lessons` (list of dict): Each dict with:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `lesson_id` (int)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `title` (str)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `completed` (bool)<br>`current_lesson` (dict): title, content (str) |
| `/mark-lesson-completed/<int:course_id>/<int:lesson_id>` | `mark_lesson_completed` | POST/GET    | Mark lesson as completed                         | Redirects back to learning page                                                                                      |
| `/assignments`            | `assignments`            | GET         | List assignments, show their status             | `assignments` (list of dict): Each dict contains:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `assignment_id` (int)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `title` (str)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `due_date` (str)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `status` (str: Pending/Submited) |
| `/submit-assignment/<int:assignment_id>` | `submit_assignment`       | GET/POST    | Show submission form or submit an assignment    | GET: `assignment` (dict): title, description (str)<br>POST: Processes submission, records grade, feedback, date      |
| `/certificates`          | `certificates`           | GET         | Display user's certificates                       | `certificates` (list of dict): Each dict has:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `certificate_id` (int)<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `username`<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `course_title`<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;- `issue_date` (str)|
| `/profile`               | `user_profile`           | GET         | View user profile form                            | `user` (dict): `email` (str), `name` (str)                                                                          |
| `/profile/update`        | `update_profile`         | POST        | Update user profile                              | Form data: `email`, `name`                                                                                          |

---

# Section 2: HTML Template Specifications

Nine templates are defined, each with exact element IDs and navigation as guided by Flask's `url_for` syntax.

---

## 1. Template: `dashboard.html`

- **Page Title**: Learning Dashboard
- **Main Container ID**: `dashboard-page` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - `dashboard-title` (h1): Static text "Learning Dashboard"
  - `user-message` (div): Displays `Welcome, {{ user_name }}!`
  - `enrolled-courses` (div): Lists enrolled courses in `<ul>` with progress shown as text.
  - `available-courses` (div): Contains a link with ID `available-courses-link` linking to `url_for('available_courses')`.

---

## 2. Template: `available_courses.html`

- **Page Title**: Available Courses
- **Main Container ID**: `courses-page` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - `available-courses-title` (h1)
  - `search-input` (`input` type="text", id="search-input", placeholder="Search courses...")
  - `courses-grid` (div) as a listing container (ul/li)
  - Each course entry:
    - Title in `<h3>`
    - Description in `<p>`
    - Link with ID: `view-course-{{ course.course_id }}` to `url_for('course_details', course_id=course.course_id)`
  - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` linking to `url_for('dashboard')`

---

## 3. Template: `course_details.html`

- **Page Title**: `{{ course.title }}`
- **Main Container ID**: `course-details-page` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - `course-title` (h1): Course title
  - `course-description` (div)
  - `enroll-button` (button, id="enroll-button")
    - Disabled if `enrolled` is true
    - Onclick posts to enroll route `/enroll/<course_id>`
  - If enrolled, show `enrollment-info` (div) with enrollment date and progress %
  - Button `back-to-catalog` linking to `url_for('available_courses')`

---

## 4. Template: `my_courses.html`

- **Page Title**: My Courses
- **Main Container ID**: `my-courses-page` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - `my-courses-title` (h1)
  - `courses-list` (ul)
  - Each course item:
    - Shows title and progress %
    - Button with ID format: `continue-learning-button-{{ course.course_id }}` linking to `url_for('learning_page', course_id=course.course_id)`
  - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` linking to `url_for('dashboard')`

---

## 5. Template: `learning_page.html`

- **Page Title**: Learning Page
- **Main Container ID**: `learning-container` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - `lessons-list` (ul)
  - Each lesson item:
    - `id="lesson-{{ lesson.lesson_id }}"`
    - CSS class `completed` if lesson.completed==True
    - Button with id `mark-complete-button-{{ lesson.lesson_id }}` linking to mark completion action
  - `lesson-content` (div)
    - Contains current lesson title `<h2>` and content `<p>`
  - Button `back-to-my-courses` linking to `url_for('my_courses')`

---

## 6. Template: `assignments.html`

- **Page Title**: Assignments
- **Main Container ID**: `assignments-page` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - `assignments-title` (h1)
  - `assignments-table` (table)
    - Columns: Title, Due Date, Status, Action
    - Button for pending assignment submissions with ID `submit-assignment-button-{{ assignment.assignment_id }}`
  - Button `back-to-dashboard` linking to `url_for('dashboard')`

---

## 7. Template: `assignment_submission.html`

- **Page Title**: {{ assignment.title }}
- **Main Container ID**: `assignment-submission` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - `assignment-title` (h1)
  - `assignment-description` (div)
  - `response-textarea` (`textarea` id)
  - `submit-button` (button type="submit")
  - Button `back-to-assignments` linking to `url_for('assignments')`

---

## 8. Template: `certificates.html`

- **Page Title**: Certificates
- **Main Container ID**: `certificates-page` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - `certificates-title` (h1)
  - `certificates-grid` (div)
    - Contains certificate cards
  - Button `back-to-dashboard` linking to `url_for('dashboard')`

---

## 9. Template: `user_profile.html`

- **Page Title**: User Profile
- **Main Container ID**: `user-profile-page` (div)
- **Elements**:
  - Form with method POST for profile update
  - `profile-email` (input type="email" with id `email`)
  - `profile-fullname` (input type="text" with id `name`)
  - `save-profile-button` (submit button)
  - Button `back-to-dashboard` linking to `url_for('dashboard')`

---

| `assignments.txt`| `assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_score`                               | `1|1|Final Project|Build calculator application|2024-12-15|200`          |
| `submissions.txt`| `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback`             | `1|1|john|My answers work!|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!`                     |
| `certificates.txt`| `certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date`                                             | `1|jane|1|2024-11-22`                                                    |

`lesson-content` (div): Display current lesson\n  - `mark-complete-button` (button): Marks lesson complete\n  - `back-to-my-courses` (button) linking to `url_for('my_courses')`\n- Context Variables: `lessons` (list), `current_lesson` (dict), `course_id` (int)\n\n\n### 6. assignments.html\n- **Page Title**: My Assignments\n- **Container ID**: `assignments-page` (div)\n- Elements:\n  - `url_for('dashboard')`\n- Context Variables: `assignments` (list)\n\n\n### 7. assignment_submission.html\n- **Page Title**: Submit Assignment\n- **Container ID**: `submit-page` (div)\n- Elements:\n  - `assignment-info` (div) showing assignment title and description\n  - `submission-text` (textarea) for text input\n  - `submit-button` (button) to POST submission\n  - `back-to-assignments` (button) linking to `url_for('assignments')`\n- Context Variables: `assignment` (dict)\n\n\n### 8. certificates.html\n- **Page Title**: My Certificates\n- **Container ID**: `certificates-page` (div)\n- hours|Active\n  2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active\n  3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active\n  ```\n\n### 3. types|2024-12-01|100\n  2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200\n  ```\n\n### 5. submissions.txt\n- Path: `data/submissions.txt`\n- Format: are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!\n  2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!\n  ```\n\n### 6. certificates.txt\n- Path: `data/certificates.txt`\n- Format:   [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'OnlineCourse' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'OnlineCourse' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse and enroll in courses, submit assignments, track progress, and receive certificates. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'OnlineCourse' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'OnlineCourse' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Learning Dashboard - **Overview**: Main hub displaying enrolled courses and progress. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: welcome-message** - Type: H1 - Welcome message displaying user's name.   - **ID: enrolled-courses** - Type: Div - Display of currently enrolled courses.   - **ID: browse-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to course catalog.   - **ID: my-courses-button** - Type: Button - Navigate to my courses page.  ### 2. Course Catalog Page - **Page Title**: Available Courses - **Overview**: Browse all available courses. - **Elements**:   - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search courses.   - **ID: course-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of course cards.   - **ID: view-course-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - View course details. (Repeated Element)   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.  ### 3. Course Details Page - **Page Title**: Course Details - **Overview**: Detailed information about a course including syllabus and enrollment option. - **Elements**:   - **ID: course-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course details page.   - **ID: course-title** - Type: H1 - Display of course title.   - **ID: course-description** - Type: Div - Full description of course content.   - **ID: enroll-button** - Type: Button - Button to enroll in the course.   - **ID: back-to-catalog** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to course catalog. - **Functionality**:   - Enroll button creates entry in enrollments.txt with 0% initial progress   - If already enrolled, button shows "Already Enrolled" and is disabled   - Enrollment date is recorded as current date  ### 4. My Courses Page - **Page Title**: My Courses - **Overview**: Display enrolled courses and progress. - **Elements**:   - **ID: my-courses-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my courses page.   - **ID: courses-list** - Type: Div - List of enrolled courses with progress.   - **ID: continue-learning-button-{course_id}** - Type: Button - Continue learning a course. (Repeated Element)   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.  ### 5. Course Learning Page - **Page Title**: Course Learning - **Overview**: View course content and lessons with progress tracking. - **Elements**:   - **ID: learning-page** - Type: Div - Container for the course learning page.   - **ID: lessons-list** - Type: Div - List of all lessons in the course.   - **ID: lesson-content** - Type: Div - Display of current lesson materials.   - **ID: mark-complete-button** - Type: Button - Button to mark current lesson as completed.   - **ID: back-to-my-courses** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to enrolled courses. - **Functionality**:   - Progress is calculated as (completed lessons / total lessons) × 100   - Marking lesson complete updates enrollments.txt progress field   - Course completion (100% progress) automatically generates certificate   - Lessons must be completed in sequence  ### 6. My Assignments Page - **Page Title**: My Assignments - **Overview**: View and submit assignments. - **Elements**:   - **ID: assignments-page** - Type: Div - Container for assignments page.   - **ID: assignments-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all assignments.   - **ID: submit-assignment-button-{assignment_id}** - Type: Button - Submit a pending assignment. (Repeated Element)   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Submit Assignment Page - **Page Title**: Submit Assignment - **Overview**: Submit assignment work with text responses. - **Elements**:   - **ID: submit-page** - Type: Div - Container for the assignment submission page.   - **ID: assignment-info** - Type: Div - Display of assignment title and description.   - **ID: submission-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to input text response.   - **ID: submit-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the assignment.   - **ID: back-to-assignments** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to assignments list. - **Functionality**:   - Submission creates entry in submissions.txt with status "Submitted"   - Submit date is recorded for late submission tracking   - Confirmation message displays after successful submission  ### 8. Certificates Page - **Page Title**: My Certificates - **Overview**: View earned course completion certificates. - **Elements**:   - **ID: certificates-page** - Type: Div - Container for the certificates page.   - **ID: certificates-grid** - Type: Div - Grid display of certificate cards.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard. - **Functionality**:   - Certificates are automatically generated when course progress reaches 100%   - Certificate entry is added to certificates.txt with current date   - Only completed courses appear in the grid  ### 9. User Profile Page - **Page Title**: My Profile - **Overview**: View and edit profile. - **Elements**:   - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for profile page.   - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Email input field.   - **ID: profile-fullname** - Type: Input - Full name input field.   - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Save profile changes.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'OnlineCourse' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**: `username|email|fullname` - **Example Data**:   ```   john|john@student.com|John Student   alice|alice@instructor.com|Alice Professor   jane|jane@student.com|Jane Learner   ```  ### 2. Courses Data - **File Name**: `courses.txt` - **Data Format**: `course_id|title|description|category|level|duration|status` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Python Programming|Learn Python from scratch|Programming|Beginner|40 hours|Active   2|Web Development|Build modern websites|Web|Intermediate|60 hours|Active   3|Data Science|Introduction to data analysis|Data|Advanced|80 hours|Active   ```  ### 3. Enrollments Data - **File Name**: `enrollments.txt` - **Data Format**: `enrollment_id|username|course_id|enrollment_date|progress|status` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john|1|2024-11-01|75|In Progress   2|jane|1|2024-10-15|100|Completed   3|john|2|2024-11-10|25|In Progress   ```  ### 4. Assignments Data - **File Name**: `assignments.txt` - **Data Format**: `assignment_id|course_id|title|description|due_date|max_points` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Python Basics Quiz|Complete the quiz on variables and data types|2024-12-01|100   2|1|Final Project|Build a calculator application|2024-12-15|200   ```  ### 5. Submissions Data - **File Name**: `submissions.txt` - **Data Format**: `submission_id|assignment_id|username|submission_text|submit_date|grade|feedback` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|john|My answers are...|2024-11-25|85|Good work!   2|2|jane|Here is my project...|2024-11-20|95|Excellent!   ```  ### 6. Certificates Data - **File Name**: `certificates.txt` - **Data Format**: `certificate_id|username|course_id|issue_date` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|jane|1|2024-11-22   ```
